<p dir="auto">注：6.0.0及以后的版本请使用gcc10.3的三方库进行编译</p>
<p dir="auto">现在我们已经拥有完整的openGauss代码，把它存储在以下目录中（以sda为例）。</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>/sda/openGauss-server</li>
<li>/sda/binarylibs</li>
<li>/sda/openGauss-third_party</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">编译第三方软件</h3><a id="user-content-编译第三方软件" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 编译第三方软件" href="#编译第三方软件"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">在编译openGauss之前，需要先编译openGauss依赖的开源及第三方软件。这些开源及第三方软件存储在openGauss-third_party代码仓库中，通常只需要构建一次。如果开源软件有更新，需要重新构建软件。</p>
<p dir="auto">用户也可以直接从<strong>binarylibs</strong>库中获取开源软件编译和构建的输出文件。</p>
<p dir="auto">如果你想自己编译第三方软件，请到openGauss-third_party仓库查看详情。</p>
<p dir="auto">执行完上述脚本后，最终编译和构建的结果保存在与<strong>openGauss-third_party</strong>同级的<strong>binarylibs</strong>目录下。在编译<strong>openGauss-server</strong>时会用到这些文件。</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">代码编译</h3><a id="user-content-代码编译" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 代码编译" href="#代码编译"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">使用build.sh编译代码</h4><a id="user-content-使用buildsh编译代码" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 使用build.sh编译代码" href="#使用buildsh编译代码"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">openGauss-server中的build.sh是编译过程中的重要脚本工具。该工具集成了软件安装编译和产品安装包编译功能，可快速进行代码编译和打包。。</p>
<p dir="auto">参数说明请见以下表格。</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th align="left">选项</th>
<th align="left">缺省值</th>
<th align="left">参数</th>
<th align="left">说明</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td align="left">-h</td>
<td align="left">请勿使用此选项。</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">帮助菜单。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-m</td>
<td align="left">release</td>
<td align="left">[debug | release | memcheck]</td>
<td align="left">选择目标版本。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-3rd</td>
<td align="left">${Code directory}/binarylibs</td>
<td align="left">[binarylibs path]</td>
<td align="left">指定binarylibs路径。该路径必须是绝对路径。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">--cmake</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">使用cmake方式编译。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-pkg</td>
<td align="left">请勿使用此选项。</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">将代码编译结果压缩至安装包。</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td align="left">-nopt</td>
<td align="left">请勿使用此选项。</td>
<td align="left">-</td>
<td align="left">如果使用此功能，则对鲲鹏平台的相关CPU不进行优化。</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>-m [debug | release | memcheck]</strong> 表示有三个目标版本可以选择：
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>release</strong>：生成release版本的二进制程序。此版本编译时，通过配置GCC高级优化选项，去除内核调试代码。此选项通常在生成环境或性能测试环境中使用。</li>
<li><strong>debug</strong>：表示生成debug版本的二进制程序。此版本编译时，增加了内核代码调试功能，一般用于开发自测环境。</li>
<li><strong>memcheck</strong>：表示生成memcheck版本的二进制程序。此版本编译时，在debug版本的基础上增加了ASAN功能，用于定位内存问题。</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><strong>-3rd [binarylibs path]为binarylibs</strong>的路径。默认设置为当前代码文件夹下存在<strong>binarylibs</strong>，因此如果<strong>binarylibs</strong>被移至<strong>openGauss-server</strong>中，或者在<strong>openGauss-server</strong>中创建了到<strong>binarylibs</strong>的软链接，则不需要指定此参数。但请注意，这样做的话，该文件很容易被<strong>git clean</strong>命令删除。</li>
<li>该脚本中的每个选项都有一个默认值。选项数量少，依赖简单。因此，该脚本易于使用。如果实际需要的参数值与默认值不同，请根据实际情况配置。</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">现在你已经知晓build.sh的用法，只需使用如下命令即可编译openGauss-server。</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path]"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path]
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">举例：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh       # 编译安装release版本的openGauss。需代码目录下有binarylibs或者其软链接，否则将会失败。
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs    # 编译安装debug版本的openGauss
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs --cmake    # 使用cmake方式编译代码，不加--cmake参数，默认使用make方式"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh       # 编译安装release版本的openGauss。需代码目录下有binarylibs或者其软链接，否则将会失败。
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs    # 编译安装debug版本的openGauss
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sda/binarylibs --cmake    # 使用cmake方式编译代码，不加--cmake参数，默认使用make方式
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">编译后的软件安装路径为：<strong>/sda/openGauss-server/dest</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">编译后的二进制文件路径为：<strong>/sda/openGauss-server/dest/bin</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">编译日志： <strong>make_compile.log</strong></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">使用命令编译代码</h4><a id="user-content-使用命令编译代码" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 使用命令编译代码" href="#使用命令编译代码"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">使用命令编译代码提供make和cmake两种编译方式，选择其中一种方式即可。</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>make编译方式：</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">获取对应的开源三方库二进制文件：</p>
<p dir="auto">从3.1.0分支和3.0.3 tag开始，对于不同的环境提供不同的开源三方库二进制文件。 目前社区提供Centos_x86_64, openEuler_aarch64, openEuler_x86_64三种平台的三方库二进制。
可以从对应地址下载 <a href="#%E4%B8%8B%E8%BD%BDopengauss">下载openGauss</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">配置环境变量</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="export CODE_BASE=________     # openGauss-server的路径
export BINARYLIBS=________    # binarylibs的路径
export GAUSSHOME=$CODE_BASE/dest/
export GCC_PATH=$BINARYLIBS/buildtools/________    # gcc的版本，根据三方包中对应的gcc版本进行填写即可，一般有gcc7.3或gcc10.3两种
export CC=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/gcc
export CXX=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/g++
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$GCC_PATH/gcc/lib64:$GCC_PATH/isl/lib:$GCC_PATH/mpc/lib/:$GCC_PATH/mpfr/lib/:$GCC_PATH/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin:$PATH
"><pre class="notranslate"><code>export CODE_BASE=________     # openGauss-server的路径
export BINARYLIBS=________    # binarylibs的路径
export GAUSSHOME=$CODE_BASE/dest/
export GCC_PATH=$BINARYLIBS/buildtools/________    # gcc的版本，根据三方包中对应的gcc版本进行填写即可，一般有gcc7.3或gcc10.3两种
export CC=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/gcc
export CXX=$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin/g++
export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$GCC_PATH/gcc/lib64:$GCC_PATH/isl/lib:$GCC_PATH/mpc/lib/:$GCC_PATH/mpfr/lib/:$GCC_PATH/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$GCC_PATH/gcc/bin:$PATH

</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">选择一个版本进行配置。</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>debug</strong>版本：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib
"><pre class="notranslate"><code># gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>release</strong>版本：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS=&quot;-O2 -g3&quot; --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS=&quot;-O2 -g3&quot; --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib
"><pre class="notranslate"><code># gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS="-O2 -g3" --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS="-O2 -g3" --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib

</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>memcheck</strong>版本：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check
"><pre class="notranslate"><code># gcc10.3.1版本（一般用于openEuler + ARM架构）
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.1 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check

# gcc10.3.0版本
./configure --gcc-version=10.3.0 CC=g++ CFLAGS='-O0' --prefix=$GAUSSHOME --3rd=$BINARYLIBS --enable-debug --enable-cassert --enable-thread-safety --with-readline --without-zlib --enable-memory-check

</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>[debug | release | memcheck]</strong> 表示有三个目标版本可用。</li>
<li>在<strong>ARM</strong>平台上，需要把 <strong>-D__USE_NUMA</strong> 添加至 <strong>CFLAGS</strong> 中。</li>
<li>在<strong>ARMv8.1</strong>及以上平台（如鲲鹏920），需要把 <strong>-D__ARM_LSE</strong> 添加至<strong>CFLAGS</strong>中。</li>
<li>如果<strong>binarylibs</strong>被移至<strong>openGauss-server</strong>中，或者在<strong>openGauss-server</strong>中创建了到<strong>binarylibs</strong>的软链接，则不需要指定 <strong>--3rd</strong> 参数。但请注意，这样做的话，该文件很容易被<code>git clean</code>命令删除。</li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">执行以下命令编译openGauss：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make -sj
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make install -sj"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make -sj
[user@linux openGauss-server]$ make install -sj
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">显示如下信息，表示编译和安装成功。</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="openGauss installation complete."><pre class="notranslate"><code>openGauss installation complete.
</code></pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>编译后的软件安装路径为: <strong>$GAUSSHOME</strong>。</li>
<li>编译后的二进制文件存放路径为：<strong>$GAUSSHOME/bin</strong>。</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>cmake编译方式：</strong></p>
<ol dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">获取对应的开源三方库二进制文件</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">配置环境变量</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=" #### 选择版本、平台信息
 export DEBUG_TYPE=release
 export BUILD_TUPLE=aarch64
 export GCC_VERSION=10.3.1
 ##### 导入三方库环境变量 
 export THIRD_BIN_PATH=________ 
 export JAVA_HOME=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/platform/openjdk8/${BUILD_TUPLE}/jdk/
 export PATH=${JAVA_HOME}/bin:$PATH
 export APPEND_FLAGS=&quot;-g3 -w -fPIC&quot;
 export GCCFOLDER=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/buildtools/gcc10.3
 export CC=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin/gcc
 export CXX=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin/g++
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/lib64:$GCCFOLDER/isl/lib:$GCCFOLDER/mpc/lib/:$GCCFOLDER/mpfr/lib/:$GCCFOLDER/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/kerberos/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/libcgroup/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/openssl/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/libcurl/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export PATH=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin:$PATH
 export PREFIX_HOME=________
 export GAUSSHOME=$PREFIX_HOME
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$PATH
"><pre class="notranslate"><code> #### 选择版本、平台信息
 export DEBUG_TYPE=release
 export BUILD_TUPLE=aarch64
 export GCC_VERSION=10.3.1
 ##### 导入三方库环境变量 
 export THIRD_BIN_PATH=________ 
 export JAVA_HOME=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/platform/openjdk8/${BUILD_TUPLE}/jdk/
 export PATH=${JAVA_HOME}/bin:$PATH
 export APPEND_FLAGS="-g3 -w -fPIC"
 export GCCFOLDER=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/buildtools/gcc10.3
 export CC=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin/gcc
 export CXX=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin/g++
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/lib64:$GCCFOLDER/isl/lib:$GCCFOLDER/mpc/lib/:$GCCFOLDER/mpfr/lib/:$GCCFOLDER/gmp/lib/:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/kerberos/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/libcgroup/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/openssl/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$THIRD_BIN_PATH/kernel/dependency/libcurl/comm/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export PATH=$GCCFOLDER/gcc/bin:$PATH
 export PREFIX_HOME=________
 export GAUSSHOME=$PREFIX_HOME
 export LD_LIBRARY_PATH=$GAUSSHOME/lib:$LD_LIBRARY_PATH
 export PATH=$GAUSSHOME/bin:$PATH

</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">选择一个版本进行配置</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# cmake编译版本选择由第二步中 DEBUG_TYPE 环境变量配置
mkdir cmake_build &amp;&amp; cd cmake_build
cmake .. -DENABLE_MULTIPLE_NODES=OFF -DENABLE_THREAD_SAFETY=ON -DENABLE_READLINE=ON -DENABLE_MOT=ON
# openEuler22.03或openEuler24.03版本
cmake .. -DENABLE_MULTIPLE_NODES=OFF -DENABLE_THREAD_SAFETY=ON -DENABLE_READLINE=ON -DENABLE_MOT=ON -DENABLE_OPENEULER_MAJOR=ON"><pre class="notranslate"><code># cmake编译版本选择由第二步中 DEBUG_TYPE 环境变量配置
mkdir cmake_build &amp;&amp; cd cmake_build
cmake .. -DENABLE_MULTIPLE_NODES=OFF -DENABLE_THREAD_SAFETY=ON -DENABLE_READLINE=ON -DENABLE_MOT=ON
# openEuler22.03或openEuler24.03版本
cmake .. -DENABLE_MULTIPLE_NODES=OFF -DENABLE_THREAD_SAFETY=ON -DENABLE_READLINE=ON -DENABLE_MOT=ON -DENABLE_OPENEULER_MAJOR=ON
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>注意</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>openEuler22.03和openEuler24.03版本需要加 <strong>-DENABLE_OPENEULER_MAJOR=ON</strong></li>
</ul>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">执行以下命令编译</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux cmake_build]$ make -sj &amp;&amp; make install -sj"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux cmake_build]$ make -sj &amp;&amp; make install -sj
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">编译完成</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>编译后的软件安装路径为: <strong>$GAUSSHOME</strong>。</li>
<li>编译后的二进制文件存放路径为：<strong>$GAUSSHOME/bin</strong>。</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">编译安装包</h3><a id="user-content-编译安装包" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 编译安装包" href="#编译安装包"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">请先阅读<a href="#%E4%BD%BF%E7%94%A8build.sh%E7%BC%96%E8%AF%91">使用build.sh编译</a>章节，了解build.sh的用法，以及如何使用该脚本编译openGauss。</p>
<p dir="auto">现在，只需添加一个-pkg选项，就可以编译安装包。</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path] -pkg"><pre class="notranslate"><code>[user@linux openGauss-server]$ sh build.sh -m [debug | release | memcheck] -3rd [binarylibs path] -pkg
</code></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">举例：</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sh build.sh -pkg       # 生成release版本的openGauss安装包。需代码目录下有binarylibs或者其软链接，否则将会失败。
sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sdc/binarylibs -pkg           # 生成debug版本的openGauss安装包"><pre class="notranslate"><code>sh build.sh -pkg       # 生成release版本的openGauss安装包。需代码目录下有binarylibs或者其软链接，否则将会失败。
sh build.sh -m debug -3rd /sdc/binarylibs -pkg           # 生成debug版本的openGauss安装包
</code></pre></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>生成的安装包存放目录：<strong>./package</strong>。</li>
<li>编译日志： <strong>make_compile.log</strong></li>
<li>安装包打包日志： <strong>./package/make_package.log</strong></li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">快速入门</h2><a id="user-content-快速入门" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 快速入门" href="#快速入门"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">参考<a href="https://opengauss.org/zh/docs/2.0.0/docs/Quickstart/Quickstart.html" rel="nofollow">快速入门</a>。</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">社区</h2><a id="user-content-社区" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 社区" href="#社区"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">治理</h3><a id="user-content-治理" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 治理" href="#治理"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">交流</h3><a id="user-content-交流" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 交流" href="#交流"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
